<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B>905 West Riverside 
Avenue, Suite&nbsp;311<BR>
Spokane, Washington 99201<BR>
NOTICE OF SPECIAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS<BR>
To be held October&nbsp;13, 2014  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>Dear Shareholder, </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We
are pleased to invite you to attend a Special Meeting of Shareholders (the 
"Special Meeting") of Mines Management,&nbsp;Inc. (the "Company"), which will be
held at 2:00&nbsp;p.m.
Spokane time on Tuesday, October&nbsp;13, 2014, at the Company's headquarters 
located at 905 West Riverside Avenue, Suite&nbsp;311, Spokane, Washington 99201.
The primary business of the meeting
will be to vote on the Company's proposals to: </FONT></P>
<UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp
;&nbsp;Approve
the issuance of shares of the Company's common stock, par value $0.001 per share
(the "Common Stock"), (a)&nbsp;upon conversion of the Company's Series&nbsp;B
6% Convertible Preferred Stock (the "Preferred Stock"), (b)&nbsp;in lieu of the 
cash payment of dividends on the Preferred Stock, and (c)&nbsp;upon exercise of 
the Company's Common Stock purchase
warrants (the "Warrants"), in excess of 19.99% of the number of shares of Common
Stock that were issued and outstanding on July&nbsp;25, 2014, the date the 
Preferred Stock and Warrants were issued
by the Company. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp
;&nbsp;Approve
the reduction of the Preferred Stock conversion price to equal the price at 
which the Company subsequently sells equity if the Company subsequently sells 
equity
at a price lower than the conversion price (the "Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution 
Provision"). </FONT></P>
</UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
foregoing items of business are more fully described in the proxy statement 
accompanying this notice. Only shareholders of record at the close of business 
on August&nbsp;15, 2014,
the record date fixed by the Board of Directors, are entitled to notice of, and 
to vote at, the Special Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments 
thereof. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;It
is important that your shares be represented at the Special Meeting whether or 
not you are personally able to attend. You are therefore urged to complete, 
date, and sign the
accompanying proxy card and mail it in the enclosed postage-paid envelope as 
promptly as possible. You may revoke your proxy either by delivering a later 
dated proxy card or by voting in person at the
Special Meeting. Thank you for your timely response. We look forward to seeing 
you at the Special Meeting. </FONT></P>
 <DIV style="padding:0pt;position:relative;width:100%;margin-left:0%;">
<p style="font-family:times;"></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B>Whether or not you plan to 
personally attend the Special Meeting, we encourage you to make certain you are 
represented at the Special Meeting by signing and dating the
accompanying proxy card and promptly returning it in accordance with its 
instructions. Returning your proxy card will not prevent you from voting in 
person at the Special Meeting, but will provide
assurance that your vote will be counted if you are unable to attend the Special
Meeting.</B></FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> IMPORTANT NOTICE 
REGARDING THE AVAILABILITY OF PROXY MATERIALS FOR THE SPECIAL MEETING OF 
SHAREHOLDERS TO BE HELD ON OCTOBER 13, 2014  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B>The Company's Notice of Special 
Meeting of Shareholders and Proxy Statement for the Special Meeting of 
Shareholders are available at
http://www.viewproxy.com/minesmanagement/2014sm.</B></FONT></P>

October&nbsp;13, 2014  </B></FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I>
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_LINERULETXT,NOSHADE  COLOR="#000000" SIZE="1.0PT" WIDTH="26%"

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> <A 
NAME="da71402_introduction"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_da71402_1"> </A>
<BR>  INTRODUCTION    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Proxy Statement is 
being furnished by the Board of Directors (the "Board") of Mines 
Management,&nbsp;Inc. (the "Company") to
holders of shares of the Company's common stock, par value $0.001 per share (the
"Common Stock"), in connection with the solicitation by the Board of proxies to 
be voted at a Special Meeting of
Shareholders to be held at 2:00&nbsp;p.m., Spokane time, on Tuesday, 
October&nbsp;13, 2014, at the Company's headquarters located at 905 West 
Riverside Avenue, Suite&nbsp;311, Spokane,
Washington 99201, and any postponements or adjournments thereof (the "Special 
Meeting"), for the purposes set forth in the accompanying Notice of Special 
Meeting of Shareholders. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This
Proxy Statement and proxy card are expected to be mailed to the shareholders 
commencing on or about September&nbsp;18, 2014. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="da71402_purposes_of_the_special_meeting"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_da71402_2"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  PURPOSES OF THE SPECIAL MEETING    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As stated in the 
accompany Notice of Special Meeting of Shareholders, the purpose of the Special 
Meeting
is:</FONT></P>
<UL>
<DL compact>
<DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> to vote on
a proposal to approve the issuance of shares of the Company's common stock, par 
value $0.001 per share (the
"Common Stock"), (a)&nbsp;upon conversion of the Company's Series&nbsp;B 6% 
Convertible Preferred Stock (the "Preferred Stock"), (b)&nbsp;in lieu of the 
cash payment of dividends on the
Preferred Stock, and (c)&nbsp;upon exercise of the Company's Common Stock 
purchase warrants (the "Warrants"), in excess of 19.99% of the number of shares 
of Common Stock that were issued and
outstanding on July&nbsp;25, 2014, the date the Preferred Stock and Warrants 
were issued by the Company; and </FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> to vote on
a proposal to approve the reduction of the Preferred Stock conversion price to 
equal the price at which the
Company subsequently sells equity if the Company subsequently sells equity at a 
price lower than the conversion price (the "Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution 
Provision"). </FONT></DD></DL>
</UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shareholders
will also vote on such other matters as may properly come before the Special 
Meeting or any postponements or adjournments thereof. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="da71402_voting_at_the_special_meeting"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_da71402_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  VOTING AT THE SPECIAL MEETING    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Record Date; Outstanding 
Shares.</B></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board has fixed the 
close of business on August&nbsp;15, 2014, as the
record date (the "Record Date") for the purpose of determining shareholders of 
the Company entitled to notice of and to vote at the Special Meeting. At the 
close of business on that date, the Company
had 29,613,176 issued and outstanding shares of Common Stock. As of the Record 
Date, the Company has issued 401,728 shares of Common Stock to the investor that
purchased Preferred Stock and Warrants
in the July&nbsp;25, 2014 offering pursuant to its conversion of 316 shares of 
Preferred Stock. Pursuant to the listing rules of the NYSE MKT, these shares of 
Common Stock held </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>1</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=4,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=228374,FOLIO='1',FILE='DISK131:
[14ZCH2.14ZCH71402]DA71402A.;10',USER='DTAYLOR',CD='15-SEP-2014;14:23' -->
<A NAME="page_da71402_1_2"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>by
this Investor cannot be voted on the proposals, but can be counted as present 
for purposes of determining a quorum. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Quorum.</B></FONT><FONT
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A majority of issued and outstanding shares, 
present in person or represented by proxy, will
constitute a quorum for the transaction of business at the Special Meeting. 
Proxies which are submitted but are not voted for or against any proposal 
(whether due to abstentions, broker non-votes or
otherwise) will be treated as present for all matters considered at the meeting.
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Solicitation of Proxies.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The accompanying proxy is solicited on behalf of 
the Company by its Board, and the
cost of solicitation will be borne by the Company. Following the original 
mailing of the proxies and soliciting materials, directors, officers, and 
employees of the Company may solicit proxies by
mail, telephone, facsimile, email or personal interviews. We have retained 
Alliance Advisors to assist in the solicitation of proxies at an estimated cost 
of approximately $5,000, plus reasonable
expenses. The Company may request brokers, custodians, nominees, and other 
record holders to forward copies of the proxies and soliciting materials to 
persons for whom they hold shares of the Company
and to request authority for the exercise of proxies. In such cases, the Company
will reimburse such record holders for their reasonable expenses. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Voting Procedures.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If your shares are registered directly in your 
name with Computershare Trust Company, the
Company's transfer agent, you are considered a shareholder of record with 
respect to those shares and the proxy card and voting instructions have been 
sent directly to you, and you may vote your
shares by proxy or in person at the Special Meeting. If, like many shareholders,
you hold your shares in "street name" through a broker, bank or other nominee 
rather than directly in your own name,
you may vote your shares in person at the Special Meeting only if you obtain a 
legal proxy to do so from your broker, bank or other nominee that holds your 
shares of record. Otherwise, because both
proposals are non-discretionary, meaning that the record holder cannot vote your
shares without instructions from you, you must submit voting instructions to 
your broker, bank or other nominee in
order for your vote to be counted. You will receive instructions from your 
broker, bank or other nominee that you must follow in order to have your shares 
voted. See Item&nbsp;7 below. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Voting by Proxy.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If you are a shareholder of record and you do not
personally attend the Special Meeting,
your shares can still be voted by appointing someone who will act as your 
proxyholder at the Special Meeting. You can either direct the Company 
representative to vote your proxy as you have indicated,
or you may designate any individual to attend the Special Meeting and be your 
proxyholder. To make such an appointment, simply fill in the person's name in 
the blank space provided in the enclosed
form of proxy. To vote your shares, your proxyholder must attend the Special 
Meeting. If you do not fill in the blank space in the enclosed form of proxy, 
the persons named in the form of proxy are
appointed to act as your proxyholder. Those persons are directors and/or 
officers of the Company. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Revocation of Proxy.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any proxy delivered in the accompanying form may 
be changed or revoked by the person
executing the proxy by execution of a proxy bearing a later date that is 
received by the Secretary of the Company at any time before the authority 
thereby granted is exercised, or by the attendance
and vote of such person at the Special Meeting. If you want to change or revoke 
your proxy and you hold your shares in "street name," contact your broker or the
nominee that holds your shares. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;How Proxies will be Voted.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Proxies received by the Board in the accompanying
form will be voted at the
Special Meeting as specified therein by the person giving the proxy. If the 
proxy received by the Company is properly executed but contains no specific 
voting instructions, the shares represented will
be voted in accordance with the recommendation of the Board. If you hold your 
shares in "street name," you will generally receive instructions from your 
broker or the nominee describing how to vote
your shares. If you do not instruct your broker or other nominee regarding the 
process by which to vote your shares, they may only vote your shares as they 
decide as to each matter for which </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>2</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=5,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=429515,FOLIO='2',FILE='DISK131:
[14ZCH2.14ZCH71402]DA71402A.;10',USER='DTAYLOR',CD='15-SEP-2014;14:23' -->
<A NAME="page_da71402_1_3"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>they
have discretionary authority. For purposes of Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and 
No.&nbsp;2, your broker or other nominee does not have discretionary authority 
to vote your shares unless they receive
timely instructions from you. A "broker non-vote" results when a broker or other
nominee does not have discretionary authority to vote on a particular matter 
because you have not given timely
instructions on
how the broker or other nominee should vote on that matter. Although any broker 
non-vote would be counted as present at the meeting for purposes of determining 
a quorum, it would be treated as not
voted with respect to non-discretionary matters. Accordingly, you must provide 
timely instructions on how the broker or other nominee should vote your shares. 
Otherwise, in the absence of timely
instructions from you, a broker non-vote will result as to those proposals. A 
broker non-vote will have no effect on the outcome of the proposals. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><B>8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Voting Power.</B></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shareholders of the Common Stock of the Company 
are entitled to one vote for each share held.
There is no cumulative voting. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>3</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A

<!-- COMMAND=ADD_BASECOLOR,"Black" -->
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_DEFAULTFONT,"font-family:times;" -->
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_TABLESHADECOLOR,"#CCEEFF" -->
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_STABLERULES,"border-bottom:solid #000000 1.0pt;" -->
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_DTABLERULES,"border-bottom:double #000000 2.25pt;" -->
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_SCRTABLERULES,"border-bottom:solid #000000 1.0pt;margin-

</FONT> <FONT SIZE=2>
<A HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A> </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> <A NAME="pro_1"></A>PROPOSAL NO. 
1&#151;APPROVAL OF THE ISSUANCE OF SHARES OF COMMON STOCK UPON THE CONVERSION OF
PREFERRED STOCK, IN LIEU OF CASH
DIVIDENDS ON PREFERRED STOCK, AND UPON EXERCISE OF WARRANTS, IN EXCESS 
OF&nbsp;19.99% OF THE NUMBER OF ISSUED AND OUTSTANDING SHARES OF COMMON STOCK ON
JULY 25, 2014  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Introduction  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On July&nbsp;25, 2014 
(the "Signing Date"), the Company entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement 
(the "Purchase Agreement") with
Alpha Capital Anstalt (the "Investor"), an entity with which to the knowledge of
the Company it had never participated in a prior transaction and had no prior 
relationship. On July&nbsp;30, 2014
(the "Closing Date"), pursuant to the terms of the Purchase Agreement, the 
Company issued and sold to the Investor 4,000 units (the "Units") at a purchase 
price of $1,000 per Unit, with each Unit
consisting of one share of Preferred Stock and one
warrant (the "Warrants") to purchase approximately 636 shares of Common Stock at
an exercise price of $1.0816 per share, subject to adjustment. Aggregate net 
proceeds to the Company were approximately
$3.6&nbsp;million. Subject to certain conditions, each share of Preferred Stock 
is convertible into approximately 1,271 shares of Common Stock (equivalent to a 
conversion price of $0.7866 per share
of Common Stock). Dividends are payable quarterly, and at the election of the 
Company, may be paid in the form of additional shares of Common Stock (the "PIK 
Dividends"). "Underlying Shares" means the
shares of Common Stock issued and issuable (i)&nbsp;upon conversion of the 
Preferred Stock, (ii)&nbsp;as PIK Dividends, and (iii)&nbsp;upon exercise of the
Warrants. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
terms of the Purchase Agreement, Preferred Stock and Warrants are complex, and 
we have summarized the material provisions herein. Because the information 
included herein is a
summary, it may not include a discussion of all of the provisions in which you 
are interested. The Purchase Agreement is attached as Appendix&nbsp;A to this 
Proxy Statement. The Articles of
Amendment to the Articles of Incorporation filed with the Idaho Secretary of 
State on July&nbsp;25, 2014 (the "Articles of Amendment"), setting forth all of 
the terms of the Preferred Stock, is
attached as Appendix&nbsp;B to this Proxy Statement. The Warrant is attached as 
Appendix&nbsp;C to this Proxy Statement. We encourage you to read 
Appendix&nbsp;A, B and C in their entirety. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Why the Company Needs Shareholder
Approval  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Common Stock is 
listed on the NYSE MKT and the Toronto Stock Exchange ("TSX"). Accordingly, the 
Company is subject to the listing
rules of the NYSE MKT. NYSE MKT Rule&nbsp;713(a)(ii) requires shareholder 
approval prior to the issuance of securities in connection with a transaction, 
other than a public offering, which may
result in the issuance or potential issuance of common stock (or securities 
convertible into or exercisable for common stock) equal to 20% or more of the 
common stock outstanding prior to the issuance
for less than the greater of book or market value. Even if convertible preferred
securities are issued at a premium to the then current market price of the 
common stock, this rule applies if the
conversion price is lower than the market price or subject to certain types of 
anti-dilution adjustments. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At
the Signing Date, the conversion price of the Preferred Stock ($0.7866 per 
share) was lower than the market price of the Common Stock ($0.94 per share). 
Accordingly, in order to
comply with the NYSE MKT listing rules, the right to convert the Preferred 
Stock, the Company's right to issue PIK Dividends and the right to exercise the 
Warrants are limited until shareholders
approve Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2. Under these limitations, the shares
of Preferred Stock and the Warrants are convertible and exercisable,
respectively, only if the Underlying Shares
issued do not exceed 19.99% of the issued and outstanding Common Stock on the 
Closing Date, or 5,839,368 shares (the "Cap"). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pursuant
to the Purchase Agreement, the Company is required to submit to the holders of 
its Common Stock, within 75&nbsp;days after the Closing Date, a request for 
approval of the
issuance of all of the Underlying Shares in excess of the Cap. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>4</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=7,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=116411,FOLIO='4',FILE='DISK131:
[14ZCH2.14ZCH71402]DC71402A.;7',USER='DTAYLOR',CD='15-SEP-2014;14:20' -->
<A NAME="page_dc71402_1_5"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Certain Consequences if the 
Proposals are Approved  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Both Proposal No.&nbsp;1 
and Proposal No.&nbsp;2 must be approved in order for the Cap to be lifted. If 
shareholders approve
Proposal No.&nbsp;1, but reject Proposal No.&nbsp;2, or, alternatively, approve 
Proposal No.&nbsp;2 but reject Proposal No.&nbsp;1, the Company will still be 
subject to the Cap, and will be
prohibited from selling any Common Stock (or any security convertible into 
Common Stock) at a lower price per share than the then existing Preferred Stock 
conversion price until both proposals are
approved. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
consequences of approval of Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 are significant,
particularly in light of the terms of the Preferred Stock. The antidilution 
provisions of the
Preferred Stock include the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision that would 
reduce the conversion price of the Preferred Stock if at any time the Company 
issues equity or equity equivalent securities
having an effective issue, exercise or conversion price lower than the then-
existing Preferred Stock conversion price. Such issuances include any sale or 
other disposition of Common Stock, any grant
of an option to purchase Common Stock, any grant of a right to reprice Common 
Stock, or any issuance of a security convertible into or exercisable for Common 
Stock with a conversion or exercise price
lower than the Preferred Stock conversion price. At the time of such an 
issuance, the Preferred Stock conversion price would be reduced to equal the 
issue, exercise or conversion price of the newly
issued security. For example, if the Company subsequently issues shares of its 
Common Stock at $0.50 per share, the conversion price of the Preferred Stock 
would be automatically reduced to $0.50 per
share. Accordingly, until all of the Preferred Stock has been converted or the 
Company has forced conversion (see Proposal No.&nbsp;1&#151;Terms of Preferred 
Stock), if the Company at any
time issues Common Stock or common stock equivalents at a price lower than the 
then conversion price (currently $0.7866), the Preferred Stock conversion price 
will adjust downward. For example, at the
Closing Date, the Preferred Stock was convertible into 5,085,176 shares of 
Common Stock. If the Company subsequently issued Common Stock for $0.50 per 
share, the Preferred Stock would be convertible
into 8,000,000 shares of Common Stock. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
PIK Dividend provision has similar consequences. The Company is obligated to pay
a 6% quarterly dividend on the Preferred Stock, and has the option to pay such 
dividend in Common
Stock, valued at the lesser of (a)&nbsp;the conversion price or (b)&nbsp;95% of 
the lesser of (i)&nbsp;the average of the volume weighted average prices (the 
"VWAPs") of the Common Stock for the
20 consecutive trading days ending on the trading day that is immediately prior 
to the applicable dividend payment date or (ii)&nbsp;the average of the VWAPs 
for the 20 consecutive trading days
ending on the trading day that is immediately prior to the date the applicable 
shares of Common Stock are issued and delivered if such delivery is after the 
dividend payment date. If a quarterly PIK
Dividend were paid on all of the originally issued Preferred Stock on 
August&nbsp;8, 2014, the Company would be required to issue 76,278
shares of Common Stock based upon the conversion price of the Preferred Stock. 
The number of shares issuable would increase if the stock price decreased. By 
approving Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and
No.&nbsp;2, shareholders are approving the issuance of an unlimited number of 
Underlying Shares. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Finally,
the issuance of Common Stock in excess of the Cap, whether on exercise of the 
Preferred Stock, exercise of Warrants or issuance of PIK Dividends, will further
dilute the voting
and other rights of holders of Common Stock, including reducing the amount that 
would be received on a liquidation of the Company. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Certain Consequences if the 
Proposals are Not Approved  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If Proposals No.&nbsp;1 
and No.&nbsp;2 are not approved, (i)&nbsp;the Preferred Stock and the Warrants 
remain subject to the Cap,
(2)&nbsp;the Company is required to seek a shareholder vote on Proposals 
No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 every three months until shareholder approval is 
obtained or the Preferred Stock is no longer
outstanding, and (3)&nbsp;the Company is prohibited from making any issuance of 
Common Stock or common stock equivalents that would result in any adjustment to 
the conversion price of the Preferred
Stock. In addition, if the Investor requested conversion of all of its Preferred
Stock and due to the Cap </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>5</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=2,SEQ=8,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT,

<A NAME="page_dc71402_1_6"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>the
Company was unable to deliver all of the conversion shares, the Company would be
required to redeem all of the then outstanding Preferred Stock for a redemption 
price, in cash, equal to 115% of
the stated value of the Preferred Stock, or a maximum of $4,600,000. If the 
Company had insufficient cash to pay the redemption and carry on its business, 
this redemption obligation could force the
Company into insolvency and bankruptcy. In any reorganization of the Company 
under Chapter&nbsp;11 of the United States Bankruptcy Code or sale of Company 
assets under Chapter&nbsp;7 of the United
States Bankruptcy Code, the Investor would be permitted to bid in the redemption
obligation, which could discourage other bidders that could be interested in the
Company assets and reduce or eliminate
any amounts paid to holders of Common Stock. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Effects of the Transaction  
</B></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Use of Proceeds  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company plans to use 
the net proceeds from the sale of the Units (estimated at approximately 
$3.6&nbsp;million after deducting
placement agent fees and expenses and investor expenses but before deducting the
Company's offering expenses) and any proceeds that may be received from the 
exercise of the Warrants, if any (a maximum
of approximately $2.7&nbsp;million), for (i)&nbsp;the advancement of the 
permitting process for the Montanore Project and preparation for the delineation
drilling program, which will include
completion of the dewatering and rehabilitation of the Libby adit and 
(ii)&nbsp;general corporate purposes, including possible acquisition and 
exploration of new mining properties. The allocation of
proceeds dedicated to the Montanore Project will depend on the timing of 
permitting. If permitting proceeds quickly, more proceeds will be spent on 
preparation for the delineation drilling program and
less on general corporate purposes. Conversely, the longer the permitting 
process, the greater the use of proceeds for general and administrative expenses
and general corporate purposes and less that
will be available for expenses directly associated with the Montanore Project. 
</FONT></P>

 <P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Terms of the Preferred Stock  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company is authorized
to issue up to 10,000,000 shares of preferred stock, no par value per share. 
Designations, rights and
preferences of the Company's preferred stock may be determined from time to time
by the Board, without further shareholder approval. The Board authorized and 
sold 4,000 shares of preferred stock
designated as Series&nbsp;B 6% Convertible Preferred Stock. Assuming a 
conversion price of the Preferred Stock of $0.7866 per share of Common Stock, 
upon the conversion of all of the Preferred Stock
issued, 5,085,176 shares of Common Stock representing 14.8% of the Common Stock 
outstanding as of July&nbsp;30, 2014 are issuable. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Listing.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Preferred Stock is not listed on a national 
securities exchange or any other nationally recognized trading system.
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Rank.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Preferred Stock ranks above all other 
outstanding classes of stock with respect to dividend rights and liquidation
preferences. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Dividends.</I></FONT><
FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Holders of the Preferred Stock are entitled 
to receive cumulative dividends at the rate per share of 6% per annum, payable
quarterly, in
cash out of legally available funds or at the election of the Company in the 
form of Common Stock. Common Stock used to pay PIK Dividends is valued at 
</FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>9</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=12,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=554669,FOLIO='9',FILE='DISK131:
[14ZCH2.14ZCH71402]DE71402A.;3',USER='DTAYLOR',CD='15-SEP-2014;14:20' -->
<A NAME="page_de71402_1_10"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>the
lesser of (a)&nbsp;the conversion price or (b)&nbsp;95% of the lesser of 
(i)&nbsp;the average of the VWAPs of the Common Stock for the 20 consecutive 
trading days ending on the trading day
that is immediately prior to the applicable dividend payment date or 
(ii)&nbsp;the average of the VWAPs for the 20 consecutive trading days ending on
the trading day that is immediately prior to the
date the applicable Common Stock is issued and delivered if such delivery is 
after the dividend payment date. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Liquidation.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon any dissolution, liquidation or winding up, 
whether voluntary or involuntary, holders of the Preferred Stock are
entitled to
receive distributions out of the Company's assets, whether capital or surplus, 
before any distributions may be made on any other outstanding classes of stock. 
The amount received by holders of the
Preferred Stock will be equal to the stated value of the Preferred Stock ($1,000
per share of Preferred Stock), plus any accrued and unpaid dividends thereon and
any other fees or liquidated damages
then due and owing. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Conversion.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each share of Preferred Stock is convertible, at 
any time and from time to time at the option of the holder thereof, into
that number of
shares of Common Stock determined by dividing the stated value of the Preferred 
Stock by the conversion price. Each share of Preferred Stock has a stated value 
of $1,000. The conversion price
initially is $0.7866 per share of Common Stock (representing a 20% discount to 
the market price of the Common Stock on the trading day immediately preceding 
the signing of the Purchase Agreement) and
is subject to adjustment as described below under "Stock Dividends and Stock 
Splits" and "Subsequent Equity Sales." This right to convert is limited by the 
beneficial ownership limitation described
below and is currently subject to the shareholder approval limitation described 
below. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Forced 
Conversion.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the 
beneficial ownership limitation and the shareholder approval limitation 
described below, the Company
may require
each share of Preferred Stock to convert into shares of Common Stock at the 
then-existing conversion price if (i)&nbsp;the VWAP for any 30 consecutive 
trading day period exceeds 150% of the then
effective conversion price and (ii)&nbsp;the volume for each trading day during 
such period exceeds 70,000 shares of Common Stock per trading day. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Redemption:</I></FONT>
<FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon the occurrence of any of the following
events, at the election of the holder of the Preferred Stock, the Company is
required to
redeem all of the Preferred Stock then held by the holder for a redemption 
price, in cash, equal to 115% of the stated value of the Preferred Stock: 
</FONT></P>
<UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i
.&nbsp;&nbsp;the
Company fails to deliver conversion shares prior to the seventh trading day 
after such shares are required to be delivered, or the Company provides written 
notice to
any holders of the Preferred Stock, including by way of public announcement of 
the Company's intention not to comply with requests for conversion of any 
Preferred Stock; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ii.&nbs
p;&nbsp;the
Company fails to pay the amount of cash due pursuant to the penalty provision in
the Preferred Stock triggered by late delivery of conversion shares; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;iii.&nbsp;&nb
sp;the
Company fails to observe or perform any other covenant, agreement or warranty 
contained in, or otherwise commits any breach of the Purchase Agreement or any 
of the
agreements contemplated therein, and such failure or breach shall not, if 
subject to the possibility of a cure by the Company, have been cured within 30 
calendar days after the date on which written
notice of such failure or breach shall have been delivered; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;iv.&nbsp;&nbs
p;the
Company redeems more than a </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>de minimis</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2> number of securities junior to the Preferred Stock other than 
repurchases of
up to $150,000 in Common Stock or common stock equivalents from departing 
officers and directors; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;v.&nbsp
;&nbsp;the
Company is a party to a change of control transaction approved by the Board; or 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;vi.&nbsp;&nbs
p;there
shall have occurred a voluntary bankruptcy event. </FONT></P>
</UL>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shareholder 
Approval.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Company has not 
obtained shareholder approval as required by the NYSE MKT and the TSX with 
respect to the
transaction
contemplated by Purchase Agreement, then the Company may not issue a number of 
Underlying Shares in excess of the Cap, 5,839,368 shares of Common Stock. In 
addition, until the applicable shareholder
approval is obtained, the conversion price of the Preferred Stock will not be 
subject to the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision, as described in "Subsequent
Equity Sales" below, in the event the
Company issues any convertible debt or equity below the then-current conversion 
price. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Beneficial Ownership 
Limitation.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company shall not
effect any conversion of the Preferred Stock or pay any PIK Dividends, and a
holder shall have
no right to convert any portion of Preferred Stock, to the extent that, after 
giving effect to such conversion, such holder, together with such holder's 
affiliates, and any persons acting as a group
together with such holder or any such affiliate, would beneficially own in 
excess of 4.99% of the number of shares of Common Stock outstanding immediately 
after giving effect to the issuance of shares
of Common Stock upon such conversion. Beneficial ownership of the
holder and its affiliates is determined in accordance with Section&nbsp;13(d) of
the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the "Exchange Act"), and the 
rules and regulations promulgated
thereunder. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Stock Dividends and Stock 
Splits.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Company pays a 
stock dividend or otherwise makes a distribution payable in shares of Common
Stock on
outstanding shares of Common Stock or any common stock equivalents, subdivides 
or combines outstanding Common Stock, or reclassifies Common Stock, the 
Preferred Stock conversion price will be adjusted
by multiplying the then conversion price by a fraction, the numerator of which 
is the number of shares of Common Stock outstanding immediately before such 
event, and the denominator of which is the
number of shares outstanding immediately after such event. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>11</FONT></P>

Sales.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to shareholder 
approval and certain exempt issuances, if the Company sells, or grants any 
option to
purchase or

Common Stock (or any security convertible into Common Stock) at a lower price 
per share than the then existing Preferred

Offerings.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Company issues

equivalents or rights that such holder could have acquired if such holder had

Preferred Stock immediately prior to the

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pro Rata 
Distributions.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Company 
declares or makes any dividend or other distribution of its assets (or rights to
acquire its
assets) to
holders of shares of Common Stock, by way of return of capital or otherwise at 
any time after the issuance of the Preferred Stock, then, in each such case, the
holder of Preferred Stock shall be
entitled to participate in such dividend or distribution to the same extent that
the holder of the Preferred Stock would have participated therein if the holder 
had held the number of shares of Common
Stock acquirable upon complete conversion of the Preferred Stock. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Fundamental 
Transaction.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Company 
effects a "fundamental transaction", then upon any subsequent conversion of the 
Preferred Stock,
 the holder
thereof shall have the right to receive, for each share of Common Stock that 
would have been issuable upon such conversion immediately prior to the 
occurrence of the fundamental transaction, the
number of shares of the successor's or acquiring corporation's common stock, or 
Common Stock if the Company is the surviving corporation, and any additional 
consideration receivable as a result of
such fundamental transaction by a holder of the number of shares of Common Stock
into which the Preferred Stock is convertible immediately prior to such 
fundamental transaction. A "fundamental
transaction" means: (i)&nbsp;the Company, directly or indirectly, in one or more
related transactions effects any merger or consolidation of the Company with or 
into another person, (ii)&nbsp;the
Company, directly or indirectly, effects any sale, lease, license, assignment, 
transfer, conveyance or other disposition of all or substantially all of its 
assets in one or a series of related
transactions, (iii)&nbsp;any direct or indirect purchase offer, tender offer or 
exchange offer (whether by the Company or another person) is completed pursuant 
to which holders of the Common Stock
are permitted to sell, tender or exchange their shares for other securities, 
cash or property which has been accepted by the holders of 50% or more of the 
outstanding Common Stock, (iv)&nbsp;the
Company, directly or indirectly, in one or more related transactions effects any
reclassification, reorganization or recapitalization of the Common Stock or any 
compulsory share exchange pursuant to
which the Common Stock is effectively converted into or exchanged for other 
securities, cash or property, (v)&nbsp;the Company, directly or indirectly, in 
one or more related transactions
consummates a stock or share purchase agreement or other business combination 
(including, without limitation, a reorganization, recapitalization, spin-off or 
scheme of arrangement) with another person
whereby such other person acquires more than 50% of the outstanding shares of 
Common Stock (not including any shares of Common Stock held by the other person 
or other persons making or party to, or
associated or affiliated with the other persons making or party to, such stock
or share purchase agreement or other business combination). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Voting 
Rights.</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as otherwise 
provided below or as otherwise required by law, the Preferred Stock has no 
voting rights. However, as
long as any
shares of Preferred Stock are outstanding, the Company shall not, without the 
affirmative vote of the holders of a majority of the then outstanding shares of 
the Preferred Stock, (a)&nbsp;alter or
change adversely the powers, preferences or rights given to the Preferred Stock,
(b)&nbsp;authorize or create any class of stock ranking as to dividends, 
redemption or distribution of assets upon a
liquidation senior to, or otherwise </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>pari 
passu</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> with, the Preferred Stock, </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Reasons for the Recommendation  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has 
considered various capital raising alternatives over the last year to raise 
capital needed to continue the Company's
business. The Board considered the positive and negative consequences of all 
alternatives available to the Company, including the issuance of securities 
pursuant to the Purchase Agreement. The Board
recommends that the shareholders approve Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 
because such approval will (i)&nbsp;allow the Company to fulfil its obligations 
under the Preferred Stock and
Warrants, (ii)&nbsp;reduce the risk of a forced redemption of the Preferred 
Stock that could cost the Company up to approximately $4.6&nbsp;million, 
(iii)&nbsp;allow the Company to sell Common
Stock (or any security convertible into Common Stock) at a lower price per share
than the then existing Preferred Stock conversion price if necessary or 
desirable to continue to fund the Company's
business, and (iv)&nbsp;protect the Company from incurring the costs of 
soliciting the shareholders again for approval of Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and 
No.&nbsp;2 in 3&nbsp;months (and every
3&nbsp;months thereafter until shareholder approval is obtained). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Recommendation of the Board  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>The Board recommends that you vote "FOR" the approval the issuance of 
all of the Underlying Shares in excess of
19.99% of the Common Stock issued and outstanding on the Closing 
Date.</B></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> <A NAME="pro_2"></A>PROPOSAL NO. 
2&#151;APPROVAL OF REDUCING THE PREFERRED STOCK CONVERSION PRICE TO EQUAL THE 
PRICE AT WHICH THE COMPANY SUBSEQUENTLY
SELLS EQUITY IF THE COMPANY SUBSEQUENTLY SELLS EQUITY AT A PRICE LOWER THAN THE 
CONVERSION PRICE  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Introduction  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As previously described, 
on July&nbsp;25, 2014, the Company entered into the Purchase Agreement with the 
Investor. On the Closing
Date, pursuant to the terms of the Purchase Agreement, the Company issued and 
sold to the Investor 4,000 Units, at a purchase price of $1,000 per Unit, with 
each unit consisting of one share of
Preferred Stock and one Warrant to purchase approximately 636 shares of Common 
Stock at an exercise price of $1.0816 per share, subject to adjustment, for 
aggregate proceeds, before offering expenses,
of $4.0&nbsp;million. Subject to certain
conditions, each share of Preferred Stock is convertible into shares of Common 
Stock at a conversion rate of approximately 1,271 shares of Common Stock 
(equivalent to a conversion price of $0.7866 per
share of Common Stock). The antidilution provisions of the Preferred Stock 
contain the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision providing that the conversion 
price is reduced to match the issuance price
of any equity security issued by the Company having an issuance price lower than
the then-existing conversion price. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For
additional information regarding use of proceeds of the proceeds from the sale 
of the Preferred Stock, or the terms of the Preferred Stock or Warrants, see 
"Proposal
No.&nbsp;1&#151;Use of Proceeds", "Proposal No.&nbsp;1&#151;Terms of the 
Preferred Stock", and "Proposal No, 1&#151;Terms of the Warrants". </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Why the Company Needs Shareholder
Approval  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Common Stock is 
listed on the NYSE MKT and TSX. Accordingly, the Company is subject to the 
listing rules of the TSX. The TSX has
required, in order for the TSX to approve the listing of certain of the 
Underlying Shares, that the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision first be 
approved by the Company's shareholders. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Accordingly,
in order to comply with the TSX regulations, the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution 
Provision is not effective until the Company's shareholders approve Proposal 
No.&nbsp;2. Until
shareholders approve this proposal, the conversion price of the Preferred Stock 
may not be reduced in the event the Company subsequently sells Common Stock, or
common stock equivalents entitling the
purchaser to acquire Common Stock, at a lower price than the then current 
conversion price. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pursuant
to the Purchase Agreement, the Company is required to submit approval of the 
Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision to its shareholders within 75&nbsp;days 
after the Closing
Date. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Certain Consequences if the 
Proposals are Approved  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Both Proposal No.&nbsp;1 
and Proposal No.&nbsp;2 must be approved in order for the Cap to be lifted. If 
shareholders approve
Proposal No.&nbsp;1, but reject Proposal No.&nbsp;2, or, alternatively, approve 
Proposal No.&nbsp;2 but reject Proposal No.&nbsp;1, the Company will still be 
subject to the Cap, and will be
prohibited from selling any Common Stock (or any security convertible into 
Common Stock) at a lower price per share than the then existing Preferred Stock 
conversion price until both proposals are
approved. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
consequences of approval of Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 are significant,
particularly in light of the terms of the Preferred Stock. The antidilution 
provisions of the
Preferred Stock include the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision that would 
reduce the conversion price of the Preferred Stock if at any time the Company 
issues equity or equity equivalent securities
having an effective issue, exercise or conversion price lower than the then-
existing Preferred Stock conversion price. Such issuances include any sale or 
other disposition of Common Stock, any grant
of an option to purchase Common Stock, any grant of a right to reprice Common 
Stock, or any issuance of a security convertible into or </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>16</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=1,SEQ=19,EFW="2221395",CP="MINES MANAGEMENT,

<A NAME="page_dg71402_1_17"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
HREF="#bg71402a_main_toc">Table of Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>exercisable
for Common Stock with a conversion or exercise price lower than the Preferred 
Stock conversion price. At the time of such an issuance, the Preferred Stock 
conversion price would be reduced
to equal the issue, exercise or conversion price of the newly issued security. 
Accordingly, until all of the Preferred Stock has been converted or the Company 
has forced conversion (see Proposal
No.&nbsp;1&#151;Terms of Preferred Stock), if the Company at any time issues 
Common Stock or common stock equivalents at a price lower than the then 
conversion price (currently $0.7866), the
Preferred Stock conversion price will adjust downward. For example, at the 
Closing Date, the Preferred Stock was convertible into 5,085,176 shares of
Common Stock. If the Company subsequently issued
Common Stock for $0.50 per share, the Preferred Stock would be convertible into 
8,000,000 shares of Common Stock. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
PIK Dividend provision has similar consequences. The Company is obligated to pay
a 6% quarterly dividend on the Preferred Stock, and has the option to pay such 
dividend in Common
Stock, valued at the lesser of (a)&nbsp;the conversion price or (b)&nbsp;95% of 
the lesser of (i)&nbsp;the average of the volume weighted average prices (the 
"VWAPs") of the Common Stock for the
20 consecutive trading days ending on the trading day that is immediately prior 
to the applicable dividend payment date or (ii)&nbsp;the average of the VWAPs 
for the 20 consecutive trading days
ending on the trading day that is immediately prior to the date the applicable 
shares of Common Stock are issued and delivered if such delivery is after the 
dividend payment date. If a quarterly PIK
Dividend were paid on all of the originally issued Preferred Stock on 
August&nbsp;8, 2014, the Company would be required to issue 76,278 shares of 
Common Stock based upon the conversion price of the
Preferred Stock. The number of shares issuable would increase if the stock price
decreased. By approving Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2, shareholders are 
approving the issuance of an
unlimited number of Underlying Shares. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Finally,
the issuance of Common Stock in excess of the Cap, whether on exercise of the 
Preferred Stock, exercise of Warrants or issuance of PIK Dividends, will further
dilute the voting
and other rights of holders of Common Stock, including reducing the amount that 
would be received on a liquidation of the Company. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Certain Consequences if the 
Proposals are Not Approved  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If Proposals No.&nbsp;1 
and No.&nbsp;2 are not approved, (i)&nbsp;the Preferred Stock and the Warrants 
remain subject to the Cap,
(2)&nbsp;the Company is required to seek a shareholder vote on Proposals 
No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 every three months until shareholder approval is 
obtained or the Preferred Stock is no longer
outstanding, and (3)&nbsp;the Company is prohibited from making any issuance of 
Common Stock or common stock equivalents that would result in any adjustment to 
the conversion price of the Preferred
Stock. In addition, if the Investor requested conversion of all of its Preferred
Stock and due to the Cap the Company was unable to deliver all of the conversion
shares, the Company would be required
to redeem all of the then outstanding Preferred Stock for a redemption price, in
cash, equal to 115% of the stated value of the Preferred Stock, or a maximum of 
$4,600,000. If the Company had
insufficient cash to pay the redemption and carry on its business, this 
redemption obligation could force the Company into insolvency and bankruptcy. In
any reorganization of the Company under
Chapter&nbsp;11 of the United States Bankruptcy Code or sale of Company assets 
under Chapter&nbsp;7 of the United States Bankruptcy Code, the Investor would be
permitted to bid in the redemption
obligation, which could discourage other bidders that could be interested in the
Company assets and reduce or eliminate any amounts paid to holders of Common 
Stock. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Required Vote  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Approval of Proposal 
No.&nbsp;2 to approve the Full Ratchet Anti-Dilution Provision will require the 
affirmative vote of a majority
of the votes cast by the holders of our Common Stock who are present in person 
or by proxy at the Special Meeting and entitled to vote on the matter, provided 
that a quorum exists at the Special
Meeting. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>17</FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For
Proposal No.&nbsp;2, abstentions will be counted towards the vote total and will
have the same effect as a vote "AGAINST" the proposal, but broker non-votes 
(which are not
"entitled to vote" on the matter) will not be counted and will have no effect. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Reasons for the Recommendation  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has 
considered various capital raising alternatives over the last year to raise 
capital needed to continue the Company's
business. The Board considered the positive and negative consequences of all 
alternatives available to the Company, including the issuance of securities 
pursuant to the Purchase Agreement. The Board
recommends that the shareholders approve Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and No.&nbsp;2 
because such approval will (i)&nbsp;allow the Company to fulfil its obligations 
under the Preferred Stock and
Warrants, (ii)&nbsp;reduce the risk of a forced redemption of the Preferred 
Stock that could cost the Company up to approximately $4.6&nbsp;million, 
(iii)&nbsp;allow the Company to sell Common
Stock (or any security convertible into Common Stock) at a lower price per share
than the then existing Preferred Stock conversion price if necessary or 
desirable to continue to fund the Company's
business, and (iv)&nbsp;protect the Company from incurring the costs of 
soliciting the shareholders again for approval of Proposals No.&nbsp;1 and 
No.&nbsp;2 in 3&nbsp;months (and every
3&nbsp;months thereafter until shareholder approval is obtained). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Recommendation of the Board  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>The Board recommends that you vote "FOR" the approval the Full Ratchet
Anti-Dilution
Provision.</B></FONT></P>

indicated by footnote, and except for community property laws where applicable, 
the persons named in the tables below have
sole voting and investment power with respect to all shares of the Common Stock 
shown as beneficially owned by them. The percentage of beneficial ownership for 
each table is based on 29,613,176 shares

 <DIV style="padding:0pt;position:relative;text-align:left;margin-left:15%;">
 <DL compact>
<DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>(2)</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>All
shares of Common Stock underlying options included in this table are related to

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="dk71402_shareholder_proposals_for_the_2015_annual_meeting"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_dk71402_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  SHAREHOLDER PROPOSALS FOR THE 2015 ANNUAL MEETING  
<BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company will review 
shareholder proposals, including director nominations, intended to be included 
in the Company's proxy materials
for the 2015 Annual Meeting of Shareholders that are received by the Company at 
its principal executive offices no later than January&nbsp;5, 2015 (assuming 
next year's Annual Meeting is held within
thirty (30)&nbsp;days of the one-year anniversary of the 2014 Annual Meeting 
that was held on June&nbsp;12, 2014). Such proposals must be submitted in 
writing and should be sent to the attention
of the Secretary of the Company. The Company will comply with Rule&nbsp;14a-8 of
the Exchange Act with respect to any proposal that meets its requirements. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In
addition, under the terms of the Company's Bylaws, a shareholder who intends to 
present an item of business at the 2015 Annual Meeting of Shareholders, 
including director nominations
(other than a proposal submitted for inclusion in the Company's proxy 
materials), must provide notice of such business to the Company not less than 90
nor more than 120&nbsp;days prior to the date
of the 2015 Annual Meeting of Shareholders; provided, that if public disclosure 
of the date of the meeting is first made less than 100&nbsp;days prior to the 
date of the meeting, notice by the
shareholder in order to be timely must be received no later than the close of 
business on the tenth day following the day on which such public disclosure of 
the date of the meeting was made.
Accordingly, assuming public disclosure of the meeting
is made 100&nbsp;days or more prior to the date of the meeting, any notice given
by or on behalf of a shareholder pursuant to these provisions of our Bylaws (and
not pursuant to Rule&nbsp;14a-8 of
the Exchange Act) must be received no earlier than February&nbsp;12, 2015 and no
later than March&nbsp;14, 2015 (assuming that the 2015 Annual Meeting is on the 
one-year anniversary of the 2014
Annual Meeting that was held on June&nbsp;12, 2014). In addition, all notices 
must contain the additional information required by our Bylaws. Such notice 
shall be sent to Secretary, Mines
Management,&nbsp;Inc., 905&nbsp;West&nbsp;Riverside&nbsp;Avenue, Suite&nbsp;311,
Spokane, Washington 99201. </FONT></P>

<A NAME="toc_dk71402_2"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  ADDITIONAL SHAREHOLDER INFORMATION    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Where You Can Find Additional 
Information  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We file annual, quarterly
and current reports, proxy statements and other information with the SEC. Our 
SEC filings are available to
the public over the Internet at the SEC's website at </FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>www.sec.gov</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> and our website at </FONT> <FONT 
SIZE=2><I>www.minesmanagement.com</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. The SEC's website 
contains reports, proxy and
information statements and other information regarding issuers, such as us, that
file electronically with the SEC. You may also read and copy any document we 
file with the SEC at the SEC's Public Reference Room at 100&nbsp;F Street, N.E.,
Washington, D.C. 20549. You may also
obtain copies of these documents at prescribed rates by writing to the SEC. You 
may call the SEC at 1-800-SEC-0330 for further information on the operation of 
its Public Reference Room. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Householding Information  
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SEC permits companies
and intermediaries (such as brokers and banks) to satisfy delivery requirements 
for proxy statements with
respect to two or more shareholders sharing the same address by delivering a 
single proxy statement to those shareholders. This process,
which is commonly referred to as "householding," is intended to reduce the 
volume of duplicate information shareholders receive and reduce expenses for 
companies. Both the Company and some of our
intermediaries may be householding our proxy materials. Once you have received 
notice from your broker or another intermediary that they will be householding 
materials sent to your address,
householding will continue until you are notified otherwise or until you revoke 
your consent. Should you wish to receive separate copies of our proxy statement 
in the future, the Company will promptly
deliver a separate copy of this document to you if you notify us in writing at 
905 West Riverside Avenue, Suite&nbsp;311, Spokane, Washington 99201, to the 
attention of the Corporate Secretary, or
by contacting us by telephone at&nbsp;509-838-6050. If you hold your shares 
through an intermediary that is householding and you want to receive separate 
copies of our proxy statement in the future,
you should contact your bank, broker or other nominee record holder. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> Other Business  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As of the date of this 
Proxy Statement, the Board is not aware of any matters that will be presented 
for action at the Special Meeting
other than those described above. However, should other business properly be 
brought before the Special Meeting, the proxies will be voted thereon at the 
discretion of the persons acting thereunder. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

Agreement (this "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") is 
dated as of July&nbsp;25,
2014, between Mines Management,&nbsp;Inc., an Idaho corporation (the 
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), and each purchaser 
identified on the signature pages hereto (each,
including its successors and assigns, a "</FONT><FONT

SIZE=2><I>Purchasers</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). </FONT></P>

and Roth Capital Partners,&nbsp;LLC, as placement agent (the "</FONT><FONT

Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Securities 
Act</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), the Company desires
to issue and sell to each Purchaser, and each Purchaser, severally and not 
jointly, desires to purchase from the Company, securities of the Company as more
fully described in this Agreement. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

are hereby
acknowledged, the Company and each Purchaser agree as follows: </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

Company, par value $0.001 per share, and any other class of securities into 
which such
securities may hereafter be reclassified or changed. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Common Stock Equivalents</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any securities
of the Company or the Subsidiaries which would entitle the holder thereof to 
acquire at
any time Common Stock, including, without limitation, any debt, preferred stock,
right, option, warrant or other instrument that is at any time convertible into 
or exercisable or exchangeable for, or
otherwise entitles the holder thereof to receive, Common Stock. </FONT></P>

Suite&nbsp;1000, Boise, Idaho 83702. </FONT></P>

SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

ascribed to such term in the Certificate of Designation. </FONT></P>

in

SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Exempt Issuance</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means the issuance of 
(a)&nbsp;shares of Common Stock or options to employees, officers, directors or 
consultants
(provided that such issuances to consultant shall not exceed 200,000 shares in 
any 12&nbsp;month period, subject to adjustment for reverse and forward stock 
splits and the like) of the Company
pursuant to any stock or option plan duly adopted for such purpose, by a 
majority of the non-employee members of the Board of Directors or a majority of 
the members of a committee of non-employee
directors established for such purpose, (b)&nbsp;securities upon the exercise or
exchange of or conversion of any Securities issued hereunder and/or other 
securities exercisable or exchangeable for
or convertible into shares of Common Stock issued and outstanding on the date of
this Agreement, provided that such securities have not been amended since the 
date of this Agreement to increase the
number of such securities or to decrease the exercise price, exchange price or 
conversion price of such securities and (c)&nbsp;securities issued pursuant to 
acquisitions or strategic transactions
approved by a majority of the disinterested directors of the Company, provided 
that any such issuance shall only be to a Person (or to the equityholders of a 
Person) which is, itself or through its
subsidiaries, an operating company or an owner of an asset in a business 
synergistic with the business of the Company and shall provide to the Company 
additional benefits in addition to the investment
of funds, but shall not include a transaction in which the Company is issuing 
securities primarily for the purpose of raising capital or to an entity whose 
primary business is investing in securities. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

from 9:30&nbsp;a.m. (New York City time) to 4:02&nbsp;p.m. (New&nbsp;York City

Stock is not then listed or quoted for trading on the OTC&nbsp;Bulletin Board 
and if prices for the Common Stock are then reported in the "Pink Sheets"

prices), the most recent bid price per share of the Common Stock so reported, or
(d)&nbsp;in all other cases, the fair
market value of a share of Common Stock as determined by an independent 
appraiser selected in good faith by the Purchasers of a majority in interest of 
the Securities then outstanding and reasonably

Company. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="le71402_article_ii._purchase_and_sale"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_le71402_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  ARTICLE II.<BR>  PURCHASE AND SALE    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2.1</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Closing.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On the Closing Date, upon the terms and subject 
to the conditions set forth herein, substantially
concurrent with the execution and delivery of this Agreement by the parties 
hereto, the Company agrees to sell, and the Purchasers, severally and not 
jointly, agree to purchase, up to an aggregate of
$4,000,000 of units consisting of (i)&nbsp;4,000 shares of Preferred Stock with 
an aggregate Stated Value for each Purchaser equal to such Purchaser's 
Subscription Amount as set forth on the
signature page hereto executed by such Purchaser and (ii)&nbsp;Warrants as 
determined by Section&nbsp;2.2(a). As described in the Registration Statement, 
the units will not be certificated and the
Preferred Stock and the Warrants will be immediately separable and issued 
separately as provided in Section&nbsp;2.2. Each Purchaser shall deliver to the 
Company, via wire transfer or a certified
check, immediately available funds equal to its Subscription Amount, and the 
Company shall deliver to each Purchaser its respective shares of Preferred Stock
and Warrants, as determined pursuant to
Section&nbsp;2.2(a), and the Company and each Purchaser shall deliver the other 
items set forth in Section&nbsp;2.2 deliverable at the Closing. Upon 
satisfaction of the covenants and conditions
set forth in Sections&nbsp;2.2 and 2.3, the Closing shall occur at the offices 
of EGS or such other location as the parties shall mutually agree. The Company 
covenants that, if the Purchaser
delivers a Notice of Conversion (as defined in the Certificate of Designation) 
to convert any shares of Preferred Stock between the date hereof and the Closing
Date, the Company shall deliver
Conversion Shares to the Purchaser on the Closing Date in connection with such 
Notice of Conversion. </FONT></P>

incorporation, bylaws or other organizational or charter documents. Each of the

such disclosure is required by law or
Trading Market regulations, in which case the disclosing party shall promptly 
provide the other party with prior notice of such public statement or 
communication. Notwithstanding the foregoing, the
Company shall not publicly disclose the name of any Purchaser, or include the 
name of any Purchaser in any filing with the Commission or any regulatory agency
or Trading Market, without the prior
written consent of such Purchaser, except: (a)&nbsp;as required by federal 
securities law in connection with the filing of final Transaction Documents with
the Commission and (b)&nbsp;to the
extent such disclosure is required by law or Trading Market regulations, in 
which case the Company shall provide the Purchasers with prior notice of such 
disclosure permitted under this
clause&nbsp;(b). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.7</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Shareholder Rights Plan.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No claim will be made or enforced by the Company 
or, with the consent of the
Company, any other Person, that any Purchaser is an "Acquiring Person" under any
control share acquisition, business combination, poison pill (including any 
distribution under a rights agreement) or
similar anti-takeover plan or arrangement in effect or hereafter adopted by the 
Company, or that any Purchaser could be deemed to trigger the provisions of any 
such plan or arrangement, by virtue of
receiving Securities under the Transaction Documents or under any other 
agreement between the Company and the Purchasers. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.8</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Non-Public Information.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except with respect to the material terms and 
conditions of the transactions
contemplated by the Transaction Documents, the Company covenants and agrees that
neither it, nor any other Person acting on its behalf, will provide any 
Purchaser or its agents or counsel with any
information that the Company believes constitutes material non-public 
information, unless prior thereto such Purchaser shall have entered into a 
written agreement with the Company regarding the
confidentiality and use of such information. The Company understands and 
confirms that each
Purchaser shall be relying on the foregoing covenant in effecting transactions 
in securities of the Company. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4.9</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Use of Proceeds.</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;4.9</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
attached hereto, the Company shall use the net proceeds from the sale of the 
Securities hereunder for working capital purposes and shall not use such 
proceeds: (a)&nbsp;for the satisfaction of any
portion of the Company's debt (other than payment of trade payables in the 
ordinary course of the Company's business and prior practices), (b)&nbsp;for the
redemption of any Common Stock or Common
Stock Equivalents, (c)&nbsp;for the settlement of any outstanding litigation 
without the prior written consent of the Purchasers who purchased at least 67% 
in interest of the Securities then
outstanding or (d)&nbsp;in violation of FCPA or OFAC regulations. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Equal Treatment of Purchasers.</I></FONT><FONT
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No consideration (including any modification of

to a waiver or modification of any provision of this Agreement unless the same

the parties to this Agreement. For clarification purposes, this provision 
constitutes a separate right granted to each Purchaser by the Company and 
negotiated separately by each Purchaser, and is
intended for the Company to treat the Purchasers as a class and shall not in any
way be construed as the Purchasers acting in concert or as a group with respect 
to the purchase, disposition or voting
of Securities or otherwise. </FONT></P>
